```
     0x4BE0 [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdop" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
     0x4BF1 [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdop" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=200*
     0x4C00 [0x1B] RETURN
```
